The new bath is off of the sitting area/landing just outside the door to the room. It has a shower, toilet and pedestal sink. We have a whole house RainSoft water filter system.                       <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="1633">
                       <div data-reactid="1634">
                        <div data-reactid="1635">
                         The Cozy Lavender Cottage is located on a farm. 1860s Charm. A few miles down the road from the famous Jack Daniel's Distillery, and antique shopper's paradise Fayetteville, TN. Music City Nashville is a scenic drive of about an hour, and 30 miles from Huntsville, and its aerospace. The area is known for its Antebellum, Georgian, and Victorian houses, Antique Shopping, as well as the Tennessee Walking Horse and Tennessee Mules.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1636">
                         The farm at one time was owned by Civil War Hero (and brother of Jack) Wiley Daniel and his heirs. Mulberry Creek runs right by the farm and is a fun place to watch the water and have a picnic. The farm has a very park-like setting with pastoral views, wooded areas and walking trails. The farm grows lavender, vegetables, and hay. There are Navajo Churro Sheep doing the weeding, and an assortment of heirloom poultry and geese.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1637">
                         The farm is in a quiet area but with easy access to Hwy 50/55, I-64, and I-65. The nearest towns where you can shop, get groceries, and dine are Fayetteville, and Lynchburg. A fun place for a good cup of coffee and something other than BBQ is Southern Perks on the square of Lynchburg. In these smaller towns, the stores often close early so try to get there in the morning.
                        </div>

                        <div data-reactid="2076">
                         My place is a historic 1895 building that is conveniently located in downtown Pulaski and has everything you need for a comfortable stay in 2200 SF. It has 3 bedrooms, 4 beds, 2 full baths, fully equipped kitchen, laundry room, and a spacious living room. It is within 5 minutes walking distance to a grocery, pharmacy, restaurants, shopping, banks, Giles County Courthouse, City Hall, and Martin Methodist College. It's a perfect place for couples, business travelers, and families (with kids).
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="2077">
                         This is a 2 level loft apartment with the kitchen, the laundry room, and the large outdoor deck with patio furniture all located downstairs. The 3 bedrooms, 2 full bathrooms , and living room with bar area are located on the 2nd floor. The 3 bedrooms comfortably sleep 6. This beautifully renovated apartment boasts 12' ceilings and great views of downtown as well as all new furniture, bedding, and linens. For guests staying one week or more, housekeeping will come once a week to clean the apartment and to change linens making sure you are completely comfortable during your visit. This weekly housekeeping is included in the discounted weekly and monthly rates and should be scheduled upon check-in. If our longterm guests should require housekeeping more frequently, this can also be arranged for an additional fee.
